# Cross-Dataset Per-Subject Performance

> **Metrics**
> - **Acc**: Accuracy (%).
> - **Precision**: Macro precision (%). Exact where prediction-level metrics were regenerated; otherwise reported as Acc following the same balanced-binary convention used in `subject_performance.md`.
> - **F1**: Macro F1 (%). Exact where available; otherwise reported as Acc under the same balanced-binary convention.
> - **κ**: Cohen kappa.
> - `Precision/F1 source = exact` means regenerated `precision_macro` and `f1_macro`; `acc_as_precision_f1` means legacy runs did not save predictions.
